     <script type="text/javascript">
      (function($) {
                // Przestrzeń globalna;
                var JMC = JMC || {};
            
                var placeholderImageUrl = "http://img.siatkarskaliga.pl/placehold/600x360.png"; 
                var $placeholderImage = $("<img>").on("load", function() {
                    var listingMessageLimit = 12;
                    var $messageContainer = $('#visibleMessageList');
                    
                    var globalFilter = function() {
                        return $(this).index() < listingMessageLimit;
                    };
                    
                    // Ładujemy prawdziwe obrazki;
                    $('#visibleMessageList .messageItem').each(function(idx, el) {
                        var imgSrc = $(el).attr("data-imgSrc");
                        var newImg = $("<img>").on("load", function() {
                            $(el).find("img.img-message").attr("src", imgSrc); 
                        }).attr("src", imgSrc);
                    });
                    
                    // Po kliknięciu zakładki musimy przefiltorwać wyniki;
                    $('.tab-toggle-button[data-tabGroup="message"]').on("tabChanged", function(e) {
                        var messageType = $(this).attr('data-messageType');
                        var messageFilter = (messageType === 'all') ? globalFilter : '[data-messageType="' + messageType + '"]';
                        $messageContainer.isotope({
                            itemSelector: '.messageItem',
                            filter: messageFilter
                        });
                    });
                    // Po kliknięciu zakładki zmieniamy adres linku "ładuj więcej..."
                    $('.tab-toggle-button[data-tabGroup="message"]').on("tabChanged", function(e) {
                        var messageType = $(this).attr('data-messageType');
                        var hashValue = (messageType === 'all') ? '' : messageType;
                        $('a#messageLoadMoreLink').get(0).hash = hashValue;
                    });
                    
                    // Od samego początku wyświetlamy część wyników;
                    $messageContainer.isotope({
                        itemSelector: '.messageItem',
                        filter: globalFilter
                    });
                }).attr("src", placeholderImageUrl);
            })(jQuery);
     </script>

       <script type="text/javascript">
        jQuery(window).load( 

			(function($){
				if ($( '[data-tabgroup="socialmedia"] a' ).length && !$( '[data-tabgroup="socialmedia"] a' ).hasClass('active') ) {
					$( '[data-tabgroup="socialmedia"]' ).one('tabChanged',function(){
						var interval = setInterval(function(){
							if( $('#visibleFeedList').closest('.tab-group').hasClass('active') ) {
								clearInterval(interval);
								setTimeout(function(){
									$('#visibleFeedList').socialMediaIsotope({
										container: "#shuffled-list.social-media-page",
										moreClick: false,
										sortAscending: false
									});
								}, 300);
							};
							console.log('interval',interval);
						}, 100);
					});
				} else {
					$('#visibleFeedList').socialMediaIsotope({
						container: "#shuffled-list.social-media-page",
						moreClick: false,
						sortAscending: false
					});
				};
			})(jQuery)

		);
       </script>
      </div>
     </div>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(function() {
        $('.tab-toggle-button').click(function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            // Zmieniamy aktywną zakładkę;
            $('.tab-toggle-button a').removeClass('active');
            $(this).find('a').addClass('active');
            // Wyświetlamy odpowiednią grupę paneli;
            var tabGroup = $(this).attr('data-tabGroup');
            $('.tab-group').removeClass('active').filter('.tab-group-' + tabGroup).addClass('active');
            // Generujemy zdarzenie oznaczające zmianę zakładki;
            $(this).trigger("tabChanged"); 
        });
    });
   </script>

   <script>
    (function($) {
		$('.classificationMore').click(function(e){
            e.preventDefault();
		    $('[data-rowtype="classifications"]').toggle();
            if ($(this).hasClass('showLess')) {
                $(this).removeClass('showLess')
                $(this).find('.textmore').text("Wyświetl więcej");
            } else {
                $(this).addClass('showLess');
                $(this).find('.textmore').text("Wyświetl mniej");
            }
		});
	})(jQuery);

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function(){

    $.fn.ownHtml = function ownHtml() {
        return $(this).appendTo("<div />").parent().html();
    };

    // Rozszerzamy klasę daty o funkcję pozwalającą dodawać dni;
    Date.prototype.addDays = function(days) {
        var dat = new Date(this.valueOf());
        dat.setDate(dat.getDate() + days);
        return dat;
    }
    
    var JMC = window.JMC || {};
    
    JMC.currentSlide = 10;
    
    var startDateArr = "2018-06-12".replace(/\D/g, " ").split(" ");
    JMC.startDate = new Date(startDateArr[0], startDateArr[1] - 1, startDateArr[2]);
    var endDateArr = "2018-07-03".replace(/\D/g, " ").split(" ");
    JMC.endDate = new Date(endDateArr[0], endDateArr[1] - 1, endDateArr[2]);
    
    JMC.toggleMoreEvents = function(btn) {
        $eventBox = $(btn).closest('.eventBox').first();
        
        var allEventCount = + $eventBox.find(".eventList .event").length;
        var visibleEventCount = + $eventBox.find(".eventList .event:visible").length;
        
        if(allEventCount > 2) {
            if(visibleEventCount <  allEventCount) {
                // Jeśli nie wszzystkie wydarzenia były widoczne, to pokazujemy wszystkie;
                JMC.showExtraEvents($eventBox);
            } else {
                // W przeciwnym przypadku ukrywamy wszystkie, poza pierwszymi trzema;
                JMC.hideExtraEvents($eventBox);
            }
            JMC.calendarCarousel.adjustHeight();
        }
    };
    
    JMC.showExtraEvents = function($eventBox) {
        $eventBox.find(".eventList .event:hidden").show();
        $eventBox.find('button.eventToggleButton').html("zwiń");
    };
    
    JMC.hideExtraEvents = function($eventBox) {
        var count = $eventBox.find(".eventList .event").filter(":gt(1)").hide().length;
        $eventBox.find('button.eventToggleButton').html("+ " + count + " więcej");
    };
    
    
    var calendarAjaxUrl = '/ajax/home?lang=pl';
    var imageCommonPath = '//img.siatkarskaliga.pl/';

    
    JMC.calendarCarousel = JMC.Carousel.create(document.getElementsByClassName("eventCarousel"), {
        "variableHeight": true,
        "adaptiveHeight": true,
        "gapWidth": 0,
        "maxHeight": 0,
        "initialSlide": JMC.currentSlide+1,
        "leftArrowContent": '<span class="glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-left"></span>',
        "rightArrowContent": '<span class="glyphicon glyphicon-chevron-right"></span>',
        "arrowsContainer": 'container',
        "responsive": [
            {
                "breakpoint": 1290,
                "settings": {
                    "slidesToShow": 4,
                    "slidesToScroll": 4,
                }
            },
            {
                "breakpoint": 992,
                "settings": {
                    "slidesToShow": 3,
                    "slidesToScroll": 3,
                    "initialSlide": JMC.currentSlide,
                }
            },
            {
                "breakpoint": 768,
                "settings": {
                    "slidesToShow": 2,
                    "slidesToScroll": 2,
                }
            },
        ],
        "callbacks": {
            "beforeChange": function beforeChange(carousel, currentSlide, nextSlide) {
                
                var $lastSlide = carousel.getActiveSlides(nextSlide).pop();
                var lastActiveDate = new Date($lastSlide.attr("data-date"));
                lastActiveDate.setHours(0);

                while(((JMC.endDate - lastActiveDate) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)) < 10) { 
                    // Musimy doczytać informacje o kolejnych dniach, ale najpierw wstawimy brakujące slajdy;
                    (function() {
                        JMC.endDate.setDate(JMC.endDate.getDate() + 1);
                        var dateStr = JMC.endDate.toISOString().substring(0,10);
                        
                        var dayOfWeek = ["Niedziela", "Poniedziałek", "Wtorek", "Środa", "Czwartek", "Piątek", "Sobota"][JMC.endDate.getUTCDay()];
                        var calendarDay = dateStr.substring(8, 10) + "." + dateStr.substring(5, 7) + "." + dateStr.substring(0, 4)
                        
                        var $template = $('#calendarSlideTemplate')
                            .clone()
                            .removeAttr('id')
                            .find('.eventList_placeholder').html("ŁADUJĘ... ").end()
                            .find('.weekDay_placeholder').html(dayOfWeek).end()
                            .find('.calendarDay_placeholder').html(calendarDay).end()
                            .show();
                        
                        carousel.add($template, function($newSlide) {
                            $newSlide
                                .attr("data-date", dateStr)
                                .addClass("eventBox eventBox-inTheFuture jmc-carousel-slide");
                            $.post(calendarAjaxUrl, {
                                'date': dateStr,
                                'accountId' : "2"                            }, function(response) {
                                var eventListArr = JSON.parse(response);
                                var $eventList = $("<ul>").addClass('eventList');
                                
                                if(eventListArr.length > 0) {
                                    eventListArr.forEach(function(eventData, idx) {
                                        var $event = $("<li>")
                                            .addClass("event colorleftborder")
                                            .addClass("event-" + eventData.type)
                                            .addClass("account" + eventData.account);

                                        if(eventData.title) {
                                            $eventTitle = $("<h4>")
                                                .addClass('eventTitle');
                                            if(eventData.link) {
                                                $eventTitle.html("<a href='" + eventData.link + "'>" + eventData.title + "</a>");
                                            } else {
                                                $eventTitle.html(eventData.title);
                                            }
                                            $event.append($eventTitle);
                                        }
                                        if(eventData.content) {
                                            $eventContent = $("<p>")
                                                .addClass('eventContent');
                                            if(eventData.link) {
                                                $eventContent.html("<a href='" + eventData.link + "'>" + eventData.content + "</a>");
                                            } else {
                                                $eventContent.html(eventData.content);
                                            }
                                            $event.append($eventContent);
                                        }
                                        if(eventData.transmissions) {
                                            var eventTransContent = '';
                                            eventData.transmissions.forEach(function(transData) {
                                                        if (transData.logo_tv) {
                                                            eventTransContent += "<img src='" + imageCommonPath + "logosbig/" + transData.logo_tv + "' />";
                                                        } else if (transData.full_logo_tv) {
                                                            eventTransContent += "<img src='" + transData.full_logo_tv + "' />";
                                                        }
                                            });
                                            $eventTrans = $("<div>")
                                                .addClass('eventTransmissionsBox')
                                                .attr("data-toggle", "popover")
                                                .attr("data-placement", "auto left")
                                                .attr("data-trigger", "hover click")
                                                .attr("data-html", "true")
                                                .attr("data-content", eventTransContent)
                                                .text("TV");
                                            $event.append($eventTrans);
                                            $eventTrans.popover();
                                        }
                                        if(idx >= 2) {
                                            $event.hide();
                                        }
                                        $event.appendTo($eventList);
                                    });
                                    if(eventListArr.length > 2) {
                                        $button = $("<button>")
                                            .attr("type", "button")
                                            .addClass("btn btn-default eventToggleButton")
                                            .text((eventListArr.length - 2) + " więcej")
                                            .click(function() {
                                                JMC.toggleMoreEvents(this);
                                            });
                                        $newSlide.find(".eventFooter").append($button);
                                    }
                                    $newSlide
                                        .find('.eventList_placeholder')
                                        .empty()
                                        .append($eventList);
                                } else {
                                    $newSlide
                                        .find('.eventList_placeholder')
                                        .empty()
                                        .html("<div class='eventList_empty'><i>Brak wydarzeń</i></div>");
                                }
                            });
                        }, "section");
                    })();
                }
            },
        },
        "slidesToScroll": 1,
    });
    $(".eventTransmissionsBox[data-toggle='popover']").popover();
});
   </script>
   <!-- Kalendarz end -->

            $(this).find('i').toggleClass('fa-toggle-on fa-toggle-off');
        });

  <script type="text/javascript">
   (function ($) {
  'use strict';
  $('.elevator-wrapper').append('<div class="elevator"><i class="fa fa-chevron-up" aria-hidden="true"></i></div>');
  var offset = 300,
  scroll_top_duration = 700,
  $back_to_top = $('.elevator');
  $(window).scroll(function () {
    ($(this).scrollTop() > offset) ? $back_to_top.addClass('elevator-is-visible') : $back_to_top.removeClass('elevator-is-visible');
  });
  $back_to_top.on('click', function (event) {
    event.preventDefault();
    $('body,html').animate({
      scrollTop: 0
      }, scroll_top_duration
    );
  });
})(jQuery);
  </script>
